[2025-11-05T19:05:44Z] Kumar Varun: I know some people find it a bit unusual that I talk this openly here. A lot of you said this to me during members’ meet too . In fact , a lot of people  around me ( colleagues , management et al) often say that I have given  too much access and that I should keep some distance from the “audience” or “community.” ↵ But my ( slightly morbid ) response to that ( in my mind , not to them .. to them I just say “ hmmm “ ) …. after the pandemic, something shifted for me. I genuinely feel life is uncertain. It can change or end without warning, and that thought stays with me. I really don’t want to waste my time being guarded just for the sake of how it looks from outside. ↵ There are so many things I still want to read, watch, learn and understand. And there are so many interesting people I still want to talk to. I don’t want to miss out on those things because I was trying to hold myself apart. ↵ So I try to keep my life simple now. If a person or a space of any wok I do makes me feel joy or curiosity, I hold on to it. If it doesn’t, I quietly move on. Very Marie Kondo type. ↵ This group gives me that good feeling. Being  here feels easy and real. So I am here because I genuinely like being here. That’s all. ↵ PS : <note to self > should stick to voice notes . Way easier !
